< Review>
I have a PO Box here and so I'v used this office regularly for nearly 10 years. Post offices are busy and like any other busy place you either accept the long lines during busy hours, or try to go when there aren't long lines. Certain things for me haven't worked out perfectly here, but the  individuals who work behind the counter have never given me less than good service, and usually it's great, and considering how busy it is, I'd say most of the time they do a fantastic job.

I got my passport here too, and I was dreading that, but as others have said, the lady who helps with that process is wonderful. And a few times she has helped behind the counter with mail issues, and she is super nice then too.

There are lots of busy/grumpy/impatient/demanding customers, but the employees who work here keep it cool and get people through as fast as possible.

If you want a quiet post office, try a different one, cause this one is busy. But the people who work here do their best and they do a good job.</Review>

<userid>103934196092199265035</userid><username>Jim</username><Time>1543097018951< /Time><Rating>5< /Rating><review>We've stayed here a couple of times. It's a nice quiet little park just 3-4 miles outside of town. It's very clean and well maintained. There are about 28 sites on gravel. The outside rows are back in, and the inside are pull through. The sites are level and have 20, 30, and 50 amp power. Each site also has water. There is a double bay dump station easily accessible. There is a laundry and shower building just a short walk (~100 yds.) from the RV parking area. They are also very clean.
This is an Elks Park, but non-members can stay for a slightly higher rate. We are not members, and it cost us $25 a night during the off season. Elk members pay $20. During the busy season it is $5 higher.< /review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNaQumq5Q-0x_T5_ZmeFKRzu7pb4uJ0G6BzdQoC=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP7S-aKSMGI82FD8_oCd1N7Iy2tKTL8yNsoIaev=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPaGSgMui7bFWRpBX_pbuUphbuVCC_KogBfSWT0=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNXZpeLrQzhXeQMznMD506jI2E1DxKH69RLzQVa=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPTHhW8pn5lLrNznb4nT9rUrs90B7cjvA1xYDGH=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN5gt1uWAcr7tlL51WNhyLplP1pn91Tk7DZXC5X=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOizJsVwL0iMrKMtccPC8Q0Cojs13FufabR4-0m=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOuqrtdW5gRfNbiOOVpl5IIpNBymcGAVcgc-YaC=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOVU2iPhg24ezmPQNydtbSsUDby_X4P4CibQmnE=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><Response>None< /Response>< GmapID>

< Review>
I give it 5 stars because the people, the service, the place are all nearly perfect. I used this storage for 4 months for my clothes and books. It is very clean, dry, and save. There are no dusts, bugs, spiders, whatsoever. The air is fresh inside the building and there is no bad smells. There are carts for you to use and the elevator is convenient. You can easily access your room during day time and night. It is well lighted in the night. The gate is secured, and the street is save. They response to your question very fast through phone and emails.

The only one thing I would like to suggest to improve is about the metal lock. Everyone need to buy the door lock when move in, which is of a special type, and you need to bring it with you when move out. I do not think the lock can be used for anything else, therefore it is a wast of the natural resources. Is it possible to be recycled and used by another person?

< review>
Hands-down, the highlight of our day -- Clos du Val offered a personalized experience, starting with a custom-printed reservation card for our table, which we were shown to by a welcoming and attentive staff.  We enjoyed our wine tasting at a relaxed pace on a beautiful sunny patio.  We noticed that a nearby table had a more aggressive agenda, which CdV honored to make sure that the party could make their next appointment.

The wine punches above its weight--it is competitive with bottles nearly twice the price; perhaps being an original Napa winery before the famous "Paris Tasting" transformed the valley explains why!<//review>

<user_name>Leilani Paez< /user_name><Time>1474065502128<//Time><Rate>1< /Rate>< Review>
So here's my experience with this place. I'm not angry just disappointed. A couple of months ago I found myself in a bind and in need of some cash. I searched for the best pawnshop and because of the reviews I decided to go with them. At first it all seemed cool but then... I missed placed my receipt. When I first pawned my items the guy at the counter said we could just buy a copy if we lost it. which was fine since all the other pawnshops usually tell u the same. About a week ago I called them and asked and they say it was no problem I could just buy a copy like they originally said. A couple days later I went down there and the owner was ringing someone up and the chuby guy came over to help me. I told him I had lost my receipt and wanted to buy a new one he immediately stated he couldnt give me a copy but he can tell me how much was due and when. I asked him the due date and he said Oct 14, 2016 and he gave the owner a quick look. which I thought was kinda weird but whatever. I asked him how we would take it out without a receipt and he said just come back with the money and it wouldn't be  problem. As it turns out God is on my side because I found the lost receipts. it was actually due on Oct 2 not the 14!!! He straight up lied to me and the owner didn't say anything. What kind of place steals from their own customers!?! Thank God I went back and took my items out today chuby was just sitting there looking real stupid. Also, i cleaned the tv and ps4 and the games myself before pawning them. I like to keep my things looking new. When I got them back he took a really long time to get them and they looked dirty the plastic on the side of the tv was coming off. I never took it off when I purchased it, the games looked dirty and had a scratch. One of the other games was in a different box. They're not suppose to touch your things until it belongs to them. They are such a disappointment. People be careful who you make business with. We work too damn hard to get the things we own so a crooked businesses like this pawnshop can get richer off our misfortunes. Research the place before you do business not everything that shines is gold. I hope this is helpful to someone else out there thinking of pawning there belongings here.</Review>
